This release contains manually corrected word alignments and transcriptions,
and an updated dictionary.  

Word alignments were generated by using the most recent release of the
transcriptions and performing forced alignments using ISIP's Hub 5E
recognition system (which is also publicly available). These
alignments were manually reviewed for accurate discrimination
between speech and non-speech.

The released data is available at:

 http://www.isip.msstate.edu/projects/switchboard/releases/switchboard_word_alignments.tar.gz

As always, let us know if you have any questions.
